[30;1m78 | [0m[35minterfaces quickly and easily, but you don't have full control over the[0m
[30;1m79 | [0m[35mwidgets, nor can you create new widgets without modifying dialog itself.[0m
[30;1m80 | [0m[35mIf you need to do low-level stuff, you should have a look at `ncurses`_[0m
[30;1m81 | [0m[35m(cf. the ``curses`` module in the Python standard library), `blessings`_[0m
